<NARRATIVE> A living room with a worn-out couch and a coffee table cluttered with books and papers. There are two doors, one leading to the kitchen and another to the hallway. We see <Character_Name>JESSICA</Character_Name>, in her mid-twenties, sitting on the couch, staring at a piece of paper in her hand.</NARRATIVE>

<Utterance>Just a minute!</Utterance>
</Turn>

<NARRATIVE> Jessica tries to smile, but it's clear she's struggling to hold back her tears. Jenny notices and gives her a sympathetic glance before turning to leave.</NARRATIVE>
